#: click on a column heading to sort on it 

 Name                                      Null?    Type
 ----------------------------------------- -------- ----------------------------
 DIRECTIVE_ID                              NOT NULL NUMBER
 TYPE                                               VARCHAR2(16)
 ENABLED                                            VARCHAR2(3)
 STATE                                              VARCHAR2(10)
 AUTO_DROP                                          VARCHAR2(3)
 REASON                                             VARCHAR2(36)
 CREATED                                            TIMESTAMP(6)
 LAST_MODIFIED                                      TIMESTAMP(6)
 LAST_USED                                          TIMESTAMP(9)
 NOTES                                              XMLTYPE

SELECT d.dir_id,
       d.type,
       d.enabled,
       (CASE WHEN d.internal_state = 'HAS_STATS' OR d.redundant = 'YES' THEN 'SUPERSEDED'
             WHEN d.internal_state IN ('NEW', 'MISSING_STATS', 'PERMANENT') THEN 'USABLE'
             ELSE 'UNKNOWN'
         END) state,
       d.auto_drop,
       f.reason,
       d.created,
       d.last_modified,
       d.last_used,
       d.internal_state,
       d.redundant
  FROM sys."_BASE_OPT_DIRECTIVE" d,
       sys."_BASE_OPT_FINDING" f
  WHERE d.f_id = f.f_id
 ORDER BY 1;
